 jetali yah bhi nahin dekhte ki loktantr or asahmati kaa sammaan karne vaali sarkarein kitni dur tak jaakar yah kaam karti hai
 In the sixties, Hollywood actress Jane Fonda appealed to American soldiers on Hanoi radio not to participate in the war against Vietnam
 yah sidhe-sidhe deshadroh kii shrenee main aata, lekin america kii ek cameti ne mana ki fonda ne galat kiya tha, magar nateeja yah nikaala ki isse america main abhivyakti kii azaadi kaa sammaan duniya bhar main badha he
 Similarly, when jean-paul Sartre made a statement regarding the independence of Algeria, there was a demand for his arrest in France
 tab france ke raashtrapati rahe charles da gaal ne kaha tha ki france apane waltare ko giraftaar nahin kar saktaa
 But instead of listening to his writers, respecting their disagreements or tolerating them, Jaitley calls them rebels, accuses them of conspiracy, making them guilty of sponsored protest
 kehane kii zarurat nahin ki yah pravriti kis raajnneetik prashikshan se aati he
 The work of Hitler's Sakha Goebbels, who were the ideals of his paternal men in the Sangh Parivar, was something like this - to speak a lie again and again so that it would appear to be the truth
 yah kaam jetali ne philhal duusari baar kiya he
 The comments jetali kii tippanee kaa sabase vidambnaapurna vaakya yah he ki pradhanmantri lekhakon kii vaicharik ashishnutaa ke sabase bade ‘victim’ yaa shikaar rahe hai
 Jaitley snatches his full meaning from the word 'victim' from this one sentence, destroying his entire suffering
 jo sabase ‘badtareen shikaar’ he, vah is desh kaa pradhanmantri ban jaataa he
 If Modi is a Victim, a victim, a victim - then who wouldn't want to be such a Victim, such a victim, such a victim? And if Modi is all this - then what are the people burnt in the best bakery of Gujarat? Who are the people murdered in Naroda slab? What are the writers and thinkers who were murdered in the past years? Those whose books were burnt, who were threatened, who had to face the destiny of leaving the country and die in foreign lands, whose faces were soiled, what are they? yah darasal shabdon ko arthhin bana dene kii raajnneeti he
 It is a game of making society memoryless
 yah nai ‘smriti’ gadhane kaa khel he
 Arun Jaitley is not doing anything new, following the familiar politics of BJP
 desh, dharm or raajnneeti ke arth badalane kaa vah khel, jiske jariye vah satta tak pahunchane main kaamyaab rahi he
 But how long this game will remain hidden, remains to be seen
 vitt mantri kaa doosraa jhooth yah he ki ye ve log hai jo dashakon se bijepi ke peeche pade hai or 2002 ke baad pradhanmantri unki vaicharik ashishnutaa ke sabase zyaada shikaar hue hai
 If the writers and intellectuals did not criticize Narendra Modi after the horrific violence of 2002 in Gujarat, who would? And if this criticism had not happened, what would have happened to Gujarat? Again, the government attitude was more alarming than this dreadful violence
 yahaan bijepi samarthakon ke is sawaal kaa jawaab bhi jaruri he ki gujarat par bolne vaale godhra par khamosh kyon rahete hai
 Godhra was undoubtedly a very painful crime
 vah jin logon ne kiya, unako sazaa milani chahie
 But instead of sending the bodies of the slain kar sevaks in Godhra to their bereaved homes, the people who decided to have their public procession called Ahmedabad turned the entire Gujarat into a burning train for the next two months
 is rakshasi pratishodh kaa koi virodh na kare to vah buddhijivi kya, sahaj manushya hone kaa adhikari nahin he
 The truth is that this family's use of the slain boys in Godhra raised questions later
 gujarat main aise parivaar mil jate hai jinke bachche maare gaye or jinke naam par smarak banane se lekar kisi tarah kii madad pahunchane kaa apana vaada sangh parivaar bhul gaya
 The violence of 1984 is offered in defense of this violence of 2002 - one is the violence of BJP and the other of Congress
 jabaki sachai yah he ki donon ke peeche maansikta ek hi thi, or tabaka bhi ek hi tha

 yah vah daur tha, jab atal bihari vaajapeyi bijepi ko gandhivadi samaajwaad se jodne kii koshish kar rahe the or do siton tak simat kar rah gaye the
 However, return to Arun Jaitley's charge
 kya yah sach he ki lekhakon or buddhijiviyon ne dashakon se sirf bijepi kaa virodh kiya he? kya yah sach he ki ve congress or left ke agenda par kaam karte rahe hai? ve koun log the jinhone 2007 main singoor or nandigram ko lekar sipiem kaa virodh kiya? unamem ek bhi bhaajapai lekhak or samskruthikarmi nahin tha
 Even then it was Romila Thapar and still it was Irfan Habib who raised her voice against him
 mahasweta devi, sunil gangopadhyaay, jai goswami, gujarat main jinke bal khinche gaye, ve medha patkar, bengal ke hi rajyapal rahe gopalkrishna gandhi, filmkaar aparnaa sen or tapan sinha, rangakarmi shanvoli mitra or gayak kabir suman- in tamaam logon ne sipiem kii barbarta kaa tikhaa pratirodh kiya

 yah sindhu kii group bi main duusari jeet thi, jisase unhone antim chaar main bhi apni jagah pakki kii

 Sindhu did not take long to return and made the score 7-7
